{"answers": ["National Industrial Recovery Act", "NIRA"], "model_answer": "According to the provided documents, the New Deal program that limited production in industry was the National Industrial Recovery Act (NIRA), which was part of the National Recovery Administration (NRA). The NIRA aimed to stimulate economic recovery by setting codes of fair competition, establishing minimum wages and maximum hours, and providing for collective bargaining. It also included stimulus funds for the Works Progress Administration (WPA) to spend and sought to raise prices, give more bargaining power for unions, and reduce harmful competition."}

This idea was later refined and popularized by Charles Lyell in his book \"Principles of Geology\" in 1830."}
